In the Interpretations on the Rules, you'll see that phrases implying doubt are good enough (e.g. "I'm going to play another just in case"). But whatever you say, it must be obvious that your intent is to hit a provisional ball. You are not, however, obliged to look for your original ball if you donâ€™t want to, but you canâ€™t actually stop your opponent or anyone else from looking, even if most golfers would consider it good etiquette to not go looking for a ball if someone has clearly stated their desire to abandon it. But if that does happen and the ball is found, you will have to proceed using that ball even if you had declared it to be lost, as the Rules do not allow you to declare a ball lost!
